<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a> (24484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:latrine.html>latrine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lātrīna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bath.html>bath</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Coined <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paracelsus" class="extiw" title="w:Paracelsus">Paracelsus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = ***led.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> (74741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">liðr</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-ND_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-ND-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþuz</i>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">ledd</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:although.html>although</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:formerly.html>formerly</a> considered <a href = vnd.unilang:alternative.html>alternative</a> forms. Cognates <a href = vnd.unilang:include.html>include</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">liður</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lith</i>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hlið</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-ND_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-ND-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlidą</i>. Akin <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> rooted <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:root.html>root</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱley-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shelter.html>shelter</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:cover.html>cover</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***leder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a> (9176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lether</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leþrą</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*létrom</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Ledder</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">leare</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>Leder</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leather.html>leather</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leen.html>leen</a> (5423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leen.html>leen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lēn</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laihną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
